2430<h1>

24316 Best Kitchen Layout Ideas for Your Renovation</h1>

2432

2433</div>

2434</div>

2435</div>

2436</div>

2437<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aa-d-d-a-da">

2438<div>

2439<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2440<div>

2441<h6>

2442By Jessica Earley</h6>

2443

2444

2445<h6>

2446March 2, 2022</h6>

2447

2448</div>

2449</div>

2450</div>

2451</div>

2452<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-abfd-cee-f-e-ece">

2453<div>

2454<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2455<div>

2456<p>

2457Whether you&rsquo;re planning a kitchen renovation or building one in your new home, the first and most important step is sifting through all the kitchen layout ideas to find the most optimal one for your space and <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/how-much-does-a-kitchen-remodel-cost/" target="_blank">

2458budget.</a>

2459</p>

2460

2461

2462<p>

2463Throughout this guide, we will explore the pros and cons of the most common kitchen layouts and provide tips for building an accessible kitchen.</p>

2464

2465</div>

2466</div>

2467</div>

2468</div>

2473</a>

2474</div>

2477</div>

2497<div>

2498<h2>

2499The Kitchen Work Triangle</h2>

2500

2501</div>

2502</div>

2503</div>

2504</div>

2505<div class="">

2506<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW--ba-eb-fa-bddb">

2507<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW--ba-eb-fa-bddb">

2508<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

2509<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

2510<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-8__13d10 Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

2511<div class="">

2512<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-e-f---bfd">

2513<div class="merce-column-container">

2514<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-afded-fa--ac-abfee">

2515<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf afded-fa--ac-abfee-singleImageAlignment">

2516<img class="afded-fa--ac-abfee-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/uEiUQVubjEB9Xt9K2DcrzRjptjhvHUhaueZuLVBX26E/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9raXRjaGVuLXdvcmstdHJpYW5nbGUtaW1hZ2Utd2ViLmpwZw" alt="kitchen work triangle on minimalist kitchen" title="kitchen work triangle on minimalist kitchen"/>

2517</div>

2518</div>

2519</div>

2520</div>

2521</div>

2522</div>

2523<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-4__3eiub Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

2524<div class="">

2525<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-e-cc---eaef">

2526<div>

2527</div>

2528</div>

2529</div>

2530</div>

2531</div>

2532</div>

2533</div>

2534</div>

2535</div>

2536<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aff-bdab--aa-cc">

2537<div>

2538<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2539<div>

2540<p>

2541Before we get into the specific layouts available, it&rsquo;s important to understand the purpose and function of the kitchen work triangle.</p>

2542

2543

2544<p>

2545The kitchen work triangle is formed by the three main work areas of your kitchen&ndash;the food preparation zone (your counters or fridge), the washing zone (sink or dishwasher), and the cooking zone (stovetop or oven). Essentially, when your kitchen is finished, you should be able to draw metaphorical lines between the zones in the form of a triangle.</p>

2546

2547

2548<p>

2549The work triangle is all about efficiency. Each of the three zones should be no more than three or four feet from each other so you can move easily from one zone to another in just a few steps.</p>

2550

2551

2552<p>

2553The most important part of the work triangle is the relationship between the sink and the stovetop. We recommend keeping them in the same stretch of counter so you can easily bounce between your meal and the dishes while you cook.</p>

2554

2555

2556<p>

2557Though they aren&rsquo;t required in a kitchen layout, the work triangle will almost always naturally occur as you design your space. Paying close attention to your work triangle will help increase efficiency and better enjoy any kitchen layout you choose.</p>

2558

2559</div>

2560</div>

2561</div>

2562</div>

2563</div>

2564</div>

2565</div>

2566</div>

2567</div>

2568</div>

2569</div>

2570</div>

2571</div>

2572<div class="">

2573<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-bd--c-b-ddaf">

2574<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-bd--c-b-ddaf">

2575<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

2576<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

2577<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

2578<div class="">

2579<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-af-a-ff-c-ad">

2580<div class="merce-column-container">

2582<div>

2584<div>

2585<h2>

2586The 6 Best Kitchen Layouts</h2>

2587

2588</div>

2589</div>

2590</div>

2591</div>

2592<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-cd--a-b-dedb">

2593<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf cd--a-b-dedb-singleImageAlignment">

2594<img class="cd--a-b-dedb-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/cnDnMM9U3rsO5wc6ROzASigfOqk7cDNiL1APKfojj4A/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9raXRjaGVuLXdvcmstdHJpYW5nbGUtd2ViLmpwZw" alt="kitchen layouts with kitchen work triangle. Features one-wall kitchen layout, galley kitchen layout, L shaped kitchen layout, U shaped kitchen layout, Island Kitchen layout, and peninsula kitchen layout" title="kitchen layouts with kitchen work triangle. Features one-wall kitchen layout, galley kitchen layout, L shaped kitchen layout, U shaped kitchen layout, Island Kitchen layout, and peninsula kitchen layout"/>

2595</div>

2596</div>

2597<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cecb-f--bb-cec">

2598<div>

2599<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2600<div>

2601<p>

2602Now that you&rsquo;ve considered the practicality of implementing the work triangle into your kitchen, it&rsquo;s time to choose the right layout! No matter the size of the space you have to work with, you will find the right design for your kitchen with one of these 6 common kitchen layouts.</p>

2603

2604</div>

2605</div>

2606</div>

2607</div>

2608</div>

2609</div>

2628<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2629<div>

2630<h3>

26311. U-Shaped Kitchen Layout</h3>

2632

2633</div>

2634</div>

2635</div>

2636</div>

2637<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ba-e-cb-d-faccf">

2638<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ba-e-cb-d-faccf-singleImageAlignment">

2639<img class="ba-e-cb-d-faccf-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/CNvXnm9RbVoVDuRCEkhKNrzjYB6NYOdYys_-ZlEVce8/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy91LXNoYXBlZC1raXRjaGVuLXdlYi5qcGc" alt="u shaped kitchen layout" title="u shaped kitchen layout"/>

2640</div>

2641</div>

2642<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ccecd-ac-ad-e-bfeca">

2643<div>

2644<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2645<div>

2646<p>

2647A U-shaped kitchen layout is arranged just like it sounds. Cabinets and appliances are arranged along three separate walls to create a U-shape that is open on one end. This kitchen layout is best in big spaces and can accommodate the needs of large families.</p>

2648

2649

2650<p>

2651U-shaped kitchens have ample counter space and kitchen storage, making it easy for the whole family to help prep multiple aspects of a meal all at once. It&rsquo;s also one of the easiest layouts for creating an efficient work triangle.</p>

2652

2653

2654<p>

2655Many U-shaped kitchens are closed, separating the clutter of the kitchen from your dining room. It defines the space you have for eating and entertaining.</p>

2656

2657

2658<p>

2659Some homeowners like to incorporate an island into their U-shaped kitchen if their space is big enough, but this tends to interrupt the flow of the kitchen.</p>

2660

2661</div>

2662</div>

2663</div>

2664</div>

2665<div class="">

2666<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-a-bd--ba-eeebf">

2667<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-a-bd--ba-eeebf">

2668<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

2669<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

2670<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-6__2LJO_ Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

2671<div class="">

2672<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-dbffe-de--bf-baccc">

2673<div class="merce-column-container">

2674<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-afac-bc-a-baee-bd">

2675<div>

2676<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2677<div>

2678<h4>

2679 <span style="font-size:18px;">

2680<strong>

2681Pros</strong>

2682</span>

2683</h4>

2684

2685

2686<ul>

2687

2688 <li>

2689Plenty of counter space and storage</li>

2690

2691 <li>

2692Separates the kitchen from other parts of your home</li>

2693

2694 <li>

2695Allows for the optimal work triangle space</li>

2696

2697 <li>

2698Easy to organize</li>

2699

2700 <li>

2701Can be open or easily adapted into a closed kitchen</li>

2783<h3>

27842. L-Shaped Kitchen Layout</h3>

2785

2786</div>

2787</div>

2788</div>

2789</div>

2790<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-de-bd-aa-a-f">

2791<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf de-bd-aa-a-f-singleImageAlignment">

2792<img class="de-bd-aa-a-f-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/GKo-T8tR1z9N-nk0yR7i7lHHug-rd21HjXBKSCita7Y/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9sLXNoYXBlZC1raXRjaGVuLXdlYi5qcGc" alt="L shaped kitchen layout" title="L shaped kitchen layout"/>

2793</div>

2794</div>

2795<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK--cc-fa-d-dfc">

2796<div>

2797<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2798<div>

2799<p>

2800L-shaped kitchens are very similar to U-shaped kitchens, except that they are arranged in an L-shape and have cabinets and appliances installed along two walls instead of three.</p>

2801

2802

2803<p>

2804L-shaped kitchens are great for maximizing efficiency with the work triangle. Because working stations are set up on just two walls, it&#39;s easy to move between working stations in just a few steps.</p>

2805

2806

2807<p>

2808Since L-shaped kitchens are usually tucked into corners where walls meet at a 90-degree angle, they have two open ends for easy entrances and exits. This is great for busy families or entertaining guests&ndash;it&rsquo;s unlikely that you will get in each other&#39;s way!</p>

2809

2810

2811<p>

2812Open plan living is a popular homestyle right now, and L-shaped kitchens fit perfectly in this concept. Arranged along only two walls, L-shaped kitchens naturally open into the surrounding rooms. Ideally, your kitchen will open into either the dining room or living room.</p>

2813

2814</div>

2815</div>

2816</div>

2817</div>

2819<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW--efe-d--fbac">

2930<h3>

29313. Island Kitchen Layout</h3>

2932

2933</div>

2934</div>

2935</div>

2936</div>

2937<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ee-ec-b--ccc">

2938<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ee-ec-b--ccc-singleImageAlignment">

2939<img class="ee-ec-b--ccc-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/_iXHFlkKw63CSm4KqMs_k16cY6V2CQTzXSv01Swo_JU/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9pc2xhbmQta2l0Y2hlbi13ZWIuanBn" alt="Island Kitchen layout" title="Island Kitchen layout"/>

2940</div>

2941</div>

2942<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aaee-ca--ab-">

2943<div>

2944<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2945<div>

2946<p>

2947If you&#39;re looking for a kitchen with ample storage and counter space, an island kitchen is the best choice! Suited especially for large kitchens, island kitchens are typically arranged in a U-shape with a freestanding section of counterspace (also known as an island) in the middle of your kitchen.</p>

2948

2949

2950<p>

2951Kitchen islands are ideal for adding counter space and storage. Most islands include base cabinets on one side to store kitchen essentials. On the other, many islands have extended countertops to accommodate seating. Add just a few stools and you will have a great casual dining space!</p>

2952

2953

2954<p>

2955In addition to installing a kitchen sink against a wall, some homeowners choose to install a sink in their island instead. You can also put your cooking station in your island by installing a flat stove stop in it.</p>

2956

2957

2958<p>

2959Whether your island becomes a washing zone, a prep zone, or a cooking zone, you can create an efficient working triangle very easily in an island kitchen. You will want to make sure there is at least 3 feet of clearance on all sides of your island to prevent crowding and inefficient traffic flow.</p>

2960

2961

2962<p>

2963Of all the kitchen layouts, island kitchens are the best for socializing. If you have a large family or love entertaining, this may be the best layout for you!</p>

2964

3081<h3>

30824. Peninsula Kitchen Layout</h3>

3083

3084</div>

3085</div>

3086</div>

3087</div>

3088<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ef-ddb-e-bf-bbcfabf">

3089<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ef-ddb-e-bf-bbcfabf-singleImageAlignment">

3090<img class="ef-ddb-e-bf-bbcfabf-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/-9EGDjUG_qu89YamhDKJxtDf3-bkcDIppT4SaFeT1Rs/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9wZW5pbnN1bGEta2l0Y2hlbi13ZWIuanBn" alt="peninsula kitchen layout" title="peninsula kitchen layout"/>

3091</div>

3092</div>

3093<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-befdfb-d-e-bea-af">

3094<div>

3095<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3096<div>

3097<p>

3098Peninsula kitchens are popular because they have some of the same functional properties as an island kitchen but are better suited for smaller spaces.</p>

3099

3100

3101<p>

3102Like an island kitchen, peninsula kitchens feature an additional worktop, but it&rsquo;s attached to the wall instead of standing in the middle of the kitchen. This saves space because you don&rsquo;t need the 3 feet of clearance on one end.</p>

3103

3104

3105<p>

3106Peninsula kitchens create a U-shape, but differ from U-shaped kitchens because the third side is completely open and accessible from three sides. Usually, one side of the peninsula piece opens into another room.</p>

3107

3108

3109<p>

3110The peninsula worktop usually includes base cabinets for extra storage. Like an island, you can extend the opposite side of the countertop to accommodate stools and create casual seating.</p>

3111

3112</div>

3113</div>

3114</div>

3115</div>

3116<div class="">

3117<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ebeb-d-eb-afbe-cdbfce">

3119<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3120<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3121<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-6__2LJO_ Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3231<h3>

32325. Galley Kitchen Layout</h3>

3233

3234</div>

3235</div>

3236</div>

3237</div>

3238<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-fdc-b-cf-ac-dbdf">

3239<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf fdc-b-cf-ac-dbdf-singleImageAlignment">

3240<img class="fdc-b-cf-ac-dbdf-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/Z92_HNZIO5kEK6dWLlpwreIWHOcFw0X0gnoi106_Xn0/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9nYWxsZXkta2l0Y2hlbi13ZWIuanBn" alt="galley kitchen layout" title="galley kitchen layout"/>

3241</div>

3242</div>

3243<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-dab-c-b-a-aaddb">

3244<div>

3245<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3246<div>

3247<p>

3248Looking for an efficient use of space? A galley kitchen might be your best fit! This kitchen layout arranges counter tops and appliances on parallel walls with a walkway that opens into other rooms on both ends.</p>

3249

3250

3251<p>

3252Galley kitchens eliminate space that is sometimes wasted with inconvenient corner cupboards. To maximize the efficiency of the work triangle, place the sink, dishwasher, and stove on the same wall with the fridge and additional counter space on the opposite wall.</p>

3253

3254

3255<p>

3256A clear and ample walkway is critical for galley kitchens. Make sure there is at least four feet of space between the cabinets and appliances on each wall. Be careful to accommodate for open oven, fridge, or cabinet doors if possible, since they can block the walkway and prevent your family&rsquo;s movement throughout the kitchen.</p>

3257

3258</div>

3259</div>

3260</div>

3261</div>

3262<div class="">

3263<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-bad-ed--af-bded">

3264<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-bad-ed--af-bded">

3265<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3266<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3267<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-6__2LJO_ Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3268<div class="">

3269<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bfbeb-be--ac-ecaa">

3270<div class="merce-column-container">

3271<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-be-d-a-bc-cdbcd">

3272<div>

3273<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3274<div>

3275<h4>

3276 <span style="font-size:18px;">

3277<strong>

3278Pros</strong>

3279</span>

3280</h4>

3281

3282

3283<ul>

3284

3285 <li>

3286Optimized for efficiency and function</li>

3287

3288 <li>

3289Great for small spaces</li>

3290

3291 <li>

3292Cost effective</li>

3293

3294 <li>

3295Part of a closed kitchen concept</li>

3296

3297</ul>

3298

3299</div>

3300</div>

3301</div>

3302</div>

3303</div>

3304</div>

3305</div>

3306</div>

3313<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3315<h4>

3316 <span style="font-size:18px;">

3317<strong>

3318Cons</strong>

3319</span>

3320</h4>

3321

3322

3323<ul>

3324

3325 <li>

3326Can be too narrow</li>

3327

3328 <li>

3329Harder for multiple people to use it at the same time</li>

3330

3331 <li>

3332Limits storage space</li>

3333

3334</ul>

3335

3336</div>

3337</div>

3338</div>

3339</div>

3340</div>

3341</div>

3342</div>

3343</div>

3344</div>

3345</div>

3348</div>

3350</div>

3351</div>

3370<div>

3371<h3>

33726. Single-Wall or One Wall Kitchen Layout</h3>

3373

3374</div>

3375</div>

3376</div>

3377</div>

3378<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ebe--c-ee-feeece">

3379<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ebe--c-ee-feeece-singleImageAlignment">

3380<img class="ebe--c-ee-feeece-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/F7lb8Q31ljCg4VXK_oe2WBIJoUIpz7EHTJfGgI90KX4/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9vbmUtd2FsbC1raXRjaGVuLXdlYi5qcGc" alt="one wall kitchen layout" title="one wall kitchen layout"/>

3381</div>

3382</div>

3383<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-eed-f--b-aed">

3384<div>

3385<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3386<div>

3387<p>

3388In single-wall kitchens (also known as single run kitchens or one wall kitchen layouts), the counter space and appliances are arranged in a single line against one wall. This arrangement is great for small spaces when other kitchen layouts are impractical.</p>

3389

3390

3391<p>

3392It&rsquo;s recommended to have counter space on either side of each major appliance. Because less counter space is needed next to the fridge, it&rsquo;s often placed at the end of the row in single-wall kitchens. Just be sure that the fridge door opens away from the wall!</p>

3393

3394

3395<p>

3396The most important consideration to remember with this layout is the amount of storage you need. With only one wall to place cabinets, you will have to get more creative when storing all your kitchen items and food. Think vertical! Install cabinets that are floor to ceiling to make the best use of your wall space.</p>

3397

3398</div>

3399</div>

3516<div>

3517<h2>

3518Open vs. Closed Kitchens</h2>

3519

3520</div>

3521</div>

3522</div>

3523</div>

3524<div class="">

3525<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-adef--b-fe-ddccdb">

3526<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-adef--b-fe-ddccdb">

3527<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3528<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3529<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-6__2LJO_ Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3530<div class="">

3531<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-aea-ee-fd-bef-aaebdde">

3532<div class="merce-column-container">

3533<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-befcc-f-d-e-accc">

3534<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf befcc-f-d-e-accc-singleImageAlignment">

3535<img class="befcc-f-d-e-accc-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/hGITv9Ws0CCMrJdHIMieE3_yulUrtQw11YhoGunFmAo/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9vcGVuLWtpdGNoZW4td2ViLmpwZw" alt="open kitchen layout" title="open kitchen layout"/>

3536</div>

3537</div>

3538</div>

3539</div>

3540</div>

3541</div>

3542<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-6__2LJO_ Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3543<div class="">

3544<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-c-ac-ce-ca-cfbcf">

3545<div class="merce-column-container">

3546<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-fe--c-b-eaebba">

3547<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf fe--c-b-eaebba-singleImageAlignment">

3548<img class="fe--c-b-eaebba-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/y5FJRSiV_Lj5uQnEnZ6M603edenUGVe0yWzEn9ISTDc/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9jbG9zZWQta2l0Y2hlbi13ZWIuanBn" alt="closed kitchen layout" title="closed kitchen layout"/>

3549</div>

3550</div>

3551</div>

3552</div>

3553</div>

3554</div>

3555</div>

3556</div>

3557</div>

3558</div>

3559</div>

3560<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aecf-ede-f--bfdbfda">

3561<div>

3562<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3563<div>

3564<p>

3565When renovating or designing a new kitchen, you will need to decide if you want it to be opened or closed.</p>

3566

3567

3568<p>

3569<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/open-concept-kitchen-ideas/" target="_blank">

3570Open kitchens</a>

3571 are meant to have easy access and open into the dining or living room space in your home. In some concepts, the kitchen is part of a &ldquo;great room,&rdquo; which can encompass the dining space, living room, and kitchen in one completely open concept. This is great for homeowners who like to integrate the majority of their family&rsquo;s activities into one common space.</p>

3572

3573

3574<p>

3575The disadvantage is that open kitchens can make your home look cluttered and unkept if not cleaned regularly. Smells from food prep, cooking, or trash can more easily travel throughout the rest of your home.</p>

3576

3577

3578<p>

3579In contrast, closed kitchens are kept completely separate from the rest of the home. For chefs who value their privacy, this type of kitchen can become a cooking or baking sanctuary! It also separates the mess and smells from the rest of your home.</p>

3580

3581

3582<p>

3583Closed kitchens are more formal and may limit the amount of socialization you have while preparing meals and entertaining guests. They also have more limited openings, which can lead to traffic bottlenecks. It may also be more difficult to have multiple cooks in the kitchen at once.</p>

3584

3585</div>

3586</div>

3587</div>

3588</div>

3589</div>

3590</div>

3591</div>

3592</div>

3593</div>

3594</div>

3595</div>

3596</div>

3597</div>

3598<div class="">

3599<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW--cac-d-bb-cbacda">

3600<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW--cac-d-bb-cbacda">

3601<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3602<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3603<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3604<div class="">

3605<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bdfcf-cdf-bb-fbd-ab">

3606<div class="merce-column-container">

3607<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ccfff-dd--aa-abbebc">

3608<div>

3609<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3610<div>

3611<h2>

3612Universal and Accessible Kitchen Design</h2>

3613

3614</div>

3615</div>

3616</div>

3617</div>

3618<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-fcbf-ba-ca--bfaae">

3619<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf fcbf-ba-ca--bfaae-singleImageAlignment">

3620<img class="fcbf-ba-ca--bfaae-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/2vKMd8WHYWlFoqfhSRElTkOx4eLpNQU4FgVjhrDrQdQ/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9raXRjaGVuLWxheW91dC1pZGVhcy9hY2Nlc3NpYmxlLWtpdGNoZW4uanBn" alt="accessible kitchen countertops" title="accessible kitchen countertops"/>

3621</div>

3622</div>

3623<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-af--ea-ffa-d">

3624<div>

3625<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3626<div>

3627<p>

3628You may be interested in universal and accessible kitchen design if you have a family member with a disability, are caring for elderly family members, or are planning ahead for staying in your home as you age.</p>

3629

3630

3631<p>

3632The great thing is that universal kitchens follow the same principles of a standard kitchen so you can choose any layout you love and make adaptations as needed.</p>

3633

3634

3635<p>

3636Here are some of the most basic changes to consider in your universal kitchen.</p>

3637

3638</div>

3639</div>

3640</div>

3641</div>

3642<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fadf-ba-ee--efdb">

3643<div>

3644<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3645<div>

3646<ul>

3647

3648 <li>

3649<strong>

3650Pay attention to counter space around appliances. </strong>

3651Since movement between workstations may be more difficult, it&rsquo;s best to have between 18 and 24 inches of clear countertop surface on both sides of your cooktop and sink. You should have at least 24 inches to one side of your fridge and oven.</li>

3652

3653 <li>

3654<strong>

3655Lower work surfaces, light switches, and outlets.</strong>

3656 Standard counter tops are 36 inches tall. Accessible kitchens should have counters that are 30 inches tall. Outlets and light switches should be no higher than 37 inches from the floor and can even be mounted on the front of cabinets.</li>

3657

3658 <li>

3659<strong>

3660Open space under sink and cooktop for seated use.</strong>

3661 Standard kitchens typically have cabinets for storage under the sink or cooktop, but in accessible kitchens this space needs to be open (especially when designing for wheelchairs). Ensure the open space is approximately 30 inches wide, 27 inches high, and 19 inches deep.</li>

3662

3663 <li>

3664<strong>

3665Be careful with your hardware.</strong>

3666 Install easy to use pulls, touch handles, levers, and handles for cabinet doors and drawers.</li>

3667

3668 <li>

3669<strong>

3670Install cabinet doors that open wider.</strong>

3671 We recommend having 170-degree hinges on your cabinet doors.</li>

3672

3673 <li>

3674<strong>

3675Reduce height of upper cabinets.</strong>

3676 The standard height for upper cabinets is 18 inches above the counter top. For better accessibility, upper cabinets should be installed no higher than 15 inches above the counter.</li>

3677

3678 <li>

3679<strong>

3680Increase visibility.</strong>

3681 Rather than having to open your cabinets to see what&rsquo;s inside, a kitchen designed for accessibility may benefit from open shelving or cabinet doors made with clear glass. Your cooktop should also have easy-to-see, front access controls.</li>

3682

3683 <li>

3684<strong>

3685Add more rolling slides and drawers. </strong>

3686The typical shelving in your cabinets may be hard to access, especially when sitting in a wheelchair. Installing sliding shelves in your cabinets makes it easier to find all your kitchen items.</li>

3687

3688 <li>

3689<strong>

3690Upgrade your sink with ergonomic features.</strong>

3691 We recommend installing single-lever, high arc faucets with a pull-out sprayer.</li>

3692

3693</ul>

3694

3695</div>

3696</div>

3697</div>

3698</div>

3699</div>

3700</div>

3701</div>

3702</div>

3703</div>

3704</div>

3705</div>

3706</div>

3707</div>

3708<div class="">

3709<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-fd-a-b-ae-bad">

3710<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-fd-a-b-ae-bad">

3711<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3712<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3713<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3714<div class="">

3715<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-cfec-de-e-a-cecf">

3716<div class="merce-column-container">

3717<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aef-bc-d-f-eca">

3718<div>

3719<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3720<div>

3721<h2>

3722Which Layout is Best for Your Home? Questions You Should Ask Before You Choose</h2>

3723

3724</div>

3725</div>

3726</div>

3727</div>

3728<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ccadf-eac-c-aff-defbcce">

3729<div>

3730<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3731<div>

3732<p>

3733Now that you&rsquo;ve learned all about the six most common kitchen layouts and tips adapting to special needs, it&rsquo;s time to determine which layout will be best for your home. Here are some questions to answer that will help you narrow down your choice.</p>

3734

3735</div>

3736</div>

3737</div>

3738</div>

3739<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aabe-bd-e-ae-cafad">

3740<div>

3741<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3742<div>

3743<ul>

3744

3745 <li>

3746<strong>

3747Who will be using the space?</strong>

3748 Designing for the primary chefs in your home takes priority but you should also consider small children and elderly family members. It&rsquo;s also best to get input from anyone else who helps your family with cooking or cleaning.</li>

3749

3750 <li>

3751<strong>

3752How many cooks do you usually have?</strong>

3753 If you have multiple family members who like to cook together, find a layout that works efficiently for more than one person.</li>

3754

3755 <li>

3756<strong>

3757What is your lifestyle like?</strong>

3758 Do you cook often or is takeout more your style? How often do you entertain? This will help you decide the size and storage needs of your kitchen as well as whether it should be open or closed.</li>

3759

3760 <li>

3761<strong>

3762Do you need to adapt for accessibility?</strong>

3763 An increased budget may be necessary for <a href="https://vevano.com/page/custom-kitchen-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

3764custom cabinets</a>

3765, counters, and appliances to properly adapt your kitchen.</li>

3766

3767 <li>

3768<strong>

3769Will you need to do other activities outside of making and eating meals?</strong>

3770 If you have kids doing homework or need to meet work-from-home needs in your kitchen, you may want to create additional counter space and seating.</li>

3771

3772 <li>

3773<strong>

3774Do you have pets?</strong>

3775 You will want to choose a kitchen layout that has space for food and water bowls.</li>

3776

3777 <li>

3778<strong>

3779Do you want a pantry? </strong>

3780Some layouts are more suited to including a pantry than others.</li>

3781

3782 <li>

3783<strong>

3784How much storage do you need?</strong>

3785 Consider how many small appliances you need to store in addition to dishes and food. If your family is small or you don&rsquo;t cook very often, smaller layouts may be fine. But if you cook a lot or have a large family, more storage will be a priority.</li>

3786

3787</ul>

3788

3789</div>

3790</div>

3791</div>

3792</div>

3793</div>

3794</div>

3795</div>

3796</div>

3797</div>

3798</div>

3799</div>

3800</div>

3806<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3807<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3808<div class="">

3809<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-deae-d-a-bdd-fcdeaac">

3810<div class="merce-column-container">

3811<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aacc-aa-e--fad">

3813<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3814<div>

3815<h2>

3816What Are 10x10 and&nbsp;12x12 Kitchen Layouts?</h2>

3817

3818</div>

3819</div>

3820</div>

3821</div>

3822<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-afc-bb-b--fcf">

3823<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf afc-bb-b--fcf-singleImageAlignment">

3824<a href="https://vevano.com/product/50682-wl-grs-linridge-grey-shaker-10x10-kitchen-cabinets/">

3825<img class="afc-bb-b--fcf-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/izRA7nIUGMwoLmvD27NG46vNQe5iXV7qLHJbIarPn8o/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9hc3NldHMudmV2YW5vLmNvbS9Qcm9kdWN0cy9XZWJJbWFnZXMvV2lsb3JhL0xpbnJpZGdlLzUwNjgyL0ltYWdlLzUwNjgyLTEuanBn" alt="10x10 kitchen " title="10x10 kitchen "/>

3826</a>

3827</div>

3828</div>

3829<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ab-a-ab-af-cdbabbe">

3830<div>

3831<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3832<div>

3833<p>

3834As you design your kitchen, it&rsquo;s likely that you will come across 10x10 and 12x12 kitchen layouts. The 10&rsquo;x10&rsquo; layout is considered the standard dimensions of a medium-sized kitchen while the 12&rsquo;x12&rsquo; layout is a standard large kitchen.</p>

3835

3836

3837<p>

3838Most kitchens will require a designer and some customization to fit all the kitchen cabinetry you need, but 10x10 and 12x12 kitchen cabinet layouts can provide a rough estimate of the cost of cabinets for the size of your kitchen. These standard dimensions help customers can easily compare cabinet prices.</p>

3839

3840

3841<p>

3842Renovating a 10x10 kitchen layout will typically cost between $10,000 and $25,000. Upgrading a 12x12 kitchen layout ranges from $14,000 to $36,000 for a full scale remodel.</p>

3843

3844</div>

3845</div>

3846</div>

3847</div>

3848<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-BUTTON-bf--c-bfe-adb">

3849<div class="Button-module_buttonWrapper__9_k6P primary-button-wrapper merce-button-wrapper">

3850<a class="merce-button-a-tag" href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-10x10-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

3851<div style="width:100%;margin:0px" class="merce-button button Button-module_button__UZ69c">

3852Browse 10x10 Kitchen Layouts</div>

3853</a>

3854</div>

3855</div>

3856</div>

3857</div>
